# Changelog

## 2026-07-19 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.2 生产集成 P02 (知识库 /library 上线; PRODUCTION DEPLOY; product_version 0.25.0)

- ADP V0.2 生产集成第 2 个可见增量。`/library` 此前线上 404（S5-P04-T067 的 Library 一直 NOT_DEPLOYED）；本次把它作为只读视图接进线上 worker：新增 libraryPage()，数据只来自线上 cn_reviews ⨝ cn_items（你学过／在复习的条目），顶部按板块与证据态分面计数并可点击筛选（?board= / ?state=），列表给出标题→条目页、板块、发布日、原文链接、证据态、复习次数、下次复习日，并复用 P01 的关键事实芯片；导航新增「知识库」入口，路由 /library 精确匹配（不遮蔽 /item/ 与 /board/）。不新增 D1 表、不改每日流水线、不改 hero/动效/主题（T078 gate 差分比对：本 diff 未移动任何视觉契约元素）。诚实边界：T067 的完整范围是 Library+笔记+全 provenance 导出，其导出规则为 source_url/version/fetched_at/claim_evidence/license 缺一即 REFUSE，而 version 与 license 属尚未上线的 S2 版本层，故本次只交付 Library 视图，不交付笔记与导出（硬做也会被 T067 规则拒绝），更不臆造 provenance；页面文案不提笔记/版本/许可/导出。★独立对抗复核 BLOCK 抓到一个真实的免费档违规★：两条查询都会全表 SCAN cn_items（D1 不带 ANALYZE 统计，规划器从大表驱动 join），每次页面访问读约 2 倍 cn_items 行数；实测（cn_reviews 固定 500 行）1k→0.4/0.8ms、20k→4.0/4.6ms、200k→33.1/39.4ms，即 200k 条时约 40 万行/次，对 D1 免费档 5M 行/天（还要与每日 cron 及所有页面共享）意味着十几次浏览即耗尽当天预算，违反 Owner 于 T087 签署的 $0/mo 免费档基线（DIR-007），并回归了已上线的 T083（其交付物正是消除热路径全表扫描）。修复：JOIN 改 CROSS JOIN（SQLite 将左表钉为外层循环，经 ON 仍是内连接，结果集不变）；修复后计划为 SCAN r + SEARCH i USING INDEX sqlite_autoindex_cn_items_1 (id=?)，cn_items 只走主键索引查找、永不扫描；负控制（改回普通 JOIN）复现 SCAN i USING COVERING INDEX，证明该检查非空跑；复核者独立复测四／七种筛选组合结果逐字节一致、无笛卡尔积（joined rows == cn_reviews 计数），STATS/LIST 提速 48-82x，并指出该修复比声称的更有价值——它在有无 ANALYZE 统计时都钉住正确计划，而 D1 不会替你跑 ANALYZE。同时修掉一个次要问题：证据态为空时的 — 分面芯片会展示无法被筛选到的计数，已不再渲染。复核终判 CONFIRMED_SOUND（未自签）。BUILD 0864030f7dc8 -> e301f8a4c7d8；部署 adp-cloud version bfa3ac49-31a2-426c-8aaf-b0c33caf60d1（DB/R2 绑定 + cron 30 20 保留）；实时验证 build.json e301f8a4c7d8、10 路由 200（含新 /library 及其筛选）、六主题 6/6、导航「知识库」存在、/library 渲染证据态与复习徽章、P01 关键事实未回归（board1 60 芯片）；回滚 wrangler versions deploy f26dc86a。本次同时修复了从 T088 起令 Project Governance 大文件卫生审计每推必红的根因：ADP 三个超 1MB 的 canonical 治理文件由 ARXIV_CANONICAL_GOVERNANCE 保留规则（max_bytes 4MB、change_policy baseline_oid_only）覆盖，每次改动都必须把新 blob OID 登记进 reviewed_oids，而这一步一直被跳过；现登记当前 OID，并新增 tests/governance/test_adp_canonical_governance_oids.py 以不变量（前缀下每个超限文件的当前 OID 必须已登记）把该类静默 CI 失败转成本地可命名的测试失败。证据 evidence/ADP-V02-P02-LIBRARY/。release_mode PRODUCTION；D1 读取量与 cn_items 规模解耦；recurring $0/mo（DIR-007 不变）。Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

## 2026-07-19 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.2 生产集成 P01 (关键事实 Factsheet 上线; PRODUCTION DEPLOY; product_version 0.24.0)

- ADP V0.2 生产集成程序的第 1 个可见增量。诚实背景: V0.1 任务包(T009-T090)把认知系统能力建成独立工具+证据包,全部 NOT_DEPLOYED,0 个接进线上 worker,线上 ≈ T040 MVP + S7 视觉,Owner 观察『网页没有明显变化』完全正确。V0.2 把已建能力分批集成上线,每批可见/可验证/可回滚,不弄坏 MVP。本任务把 S1-P03-T016 的 extract_factsheet 确定性抽取(DOI/文号/关键数字/作者;缺失即空,绝不编造)忠实移植进 deploy/cloudflare/worker_cloud.js(新增 factsheet()+factsheetHTML()),渲染为六主题自适应 .badge 芯片,铺在今天卡(首屏)/板块列表/搜索/雷达/条目详情(复用 itemListHTML 一处覆盖 board/search/radar)。纯展示层: 只读现有 cn_items 字段,不新增 D1 表/不改每日流水线/不改 hero 动效主题(T077/T078 视觉动效契约明确 page body 不在冻结范围)。独立对抗复核 BLOCK 抓到真实 ReDoS: FS_UNIT_RE 的 \d[\d,.]*\s*(?:unit) 是 O(n²),40KB 恶意输入实测 2295ms,跑在请求路径会打爆 Cloudflare Worker CPU;双重修复——有界量词 \d[\d,.]{0,39}(数字 token 永不超 40 字符,全扫描线性)+ factsheet() 输入 slice(0,500)/slice(0,2000) 兜底;复核复验 40KB→4.8ms、400KB→48.8ms(10× 线性证明)、加 slice 0.24ms,真实数字/单位抽取不变,终判 CONFIRMED_SOUND(未自签)。BUILD 自排除哈希 452f7c5de919 -> 0864030f7dc8;部署 adp-cloud version f26dc86a-446f-445b-b1ab-d2c132b1cf46(DB/R2 绑定 + cron 30 20 保留);实时验证 build.json 0864030f7dc8、7 路由 200、六主题 6/6、factsheet 芯片 board1=60/board2=4/board3=7/board4=1 真实可见;回滚 wrangler versions deploy 5a7c0fbe(452f7c5de919)。证据 evidence/ADP-V02-P01-FACTSHEET/(TASK_REPORT/adversarial_review/cost_value/test-results,ACCEPTANCE=PASS)。release_mode PRODUCTION;成本 D1 0/0、R2 0/0、model 0、recurring $0/mo(DIR-007 free tier 不变)。Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

New tool arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/tools/soak_stopline_drill.py drills all 8 anti-black-hole stop-the-line triggers against their real detection gates, each load-bearing (fires on the trigger, not on a benign negative control): source/deploy hash drift + six-theme/motion unapproved deletion via visual_regression_ci (T078) BLOCK; no-evidence + self-signed-PASS via validate_evidence (T008); prediction time leakage via dataset_snapshot.assert_no_leakage (T070); and backfill P95 > baseline +20%, cost over the DIR-007 free-tier limit (guardFrac 0.9), and the third repeated failure via deterministic mirrors of the real thresholds. It also carries the soak monitoring framework (daily-manifest schema + 14-day accumulator + SLA/quality/cost trends). release_mode NOT_DEPLOYED (no worker/schema/source_registry change; drills run in isolation; live still serves b189d3cc0703). This task does NOT advance the completed count (stays 88/90); T089 completes only when the operator runs the daily cron for 14 consecutive days with no Sev-1/2, and T090 (final handoff) depends on that. Realtime not regressed (NOT deployed; live b189d3cc0703). Cost: production 0; recurring $0/mo. Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

## 2026-07-18 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.1 task ADP-S8-P02-T088 (feature-flagged canary framework; NOT_DEPLOYED)

- Eighty-eighth task (Stage S8 / S8-P02) of the ADP V0.1 FINAL EXECUTION program, first task after the Owner signed the T087 Value-Cost Gate. Delivers the feature-flagged CANARY FRAMEWORK -- the mechanism for opening new paths incrementally instead of a big-bang switch -- and VERIFIES it over the existing stable live worker (b189d3cc0703) without deploying anything new. New tool arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/tools/canary_framework.py parses the worker for every feature flag and proves each is a canary lever: 4 flags -- BOARD3_A0_ONLY (=false), RAW_DUALWRITE (=true, SHADOW), RUM_ENABLED (=true) and the RUM_SAMPLE dial (=1) -- are each an independent standalone flag that gates its OWN additive side path (so turning it off is a safe default that leaves the publish main chain intact and touches no other flag), each with a kill switch and a rollback path. The error-budget AUTO-STOP is anchored on the LIVE DIR-007 fail-closed budget guard (R2_BUDGET, guardFrac 0.9 -> over_budget stop), with the canary quality error-budget defined as a rule that lowers RUM_SAMPLE / disables the flag on a CWV breach (reusing each flag's kill switch as the auto-stop lever). Deliverables under evidence/ADP-S8-P02-T088/: canary_framework.json, CANARY_PLAN.md (flag inventory, cohorts, kill switches, monitoring, error-budget auto-stop, held-capability rollout), known_gaps.md (honestly scopes this as a framework+verification that deploys nothing -- a real capability canary is a per-capability Owner-gated follow-on, and the CWV quality auto-stop needs deploy-side wiring), adversarial_review.md. release_mode NOT_DEPLOYED (no worker/schema/source_registry change; framework reads the worker read-only; live still serves b189d3cc0703). Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S8-P02-T088/test-results/canary_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0): every flag independently rollback-able + kill switch + off-safe, and a fail-closed error-budget auto-stop exists; 3 load-bearing negative controls fire (removing a flag's conditional gate makes it non-independent; coupling two flags in one condition makes both non-independent; flipping over_budget:true breaks the auto-stop detection). Realtime not regressed (NOT deployed; live b189d3cc0703). Cost: production 0 (NOT_DEPLOYED); recurring $0/mo (free tier); 1 read-only GET. Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

A0-official Board3, the six-theme UI/motion/a11y, and R2 raw-artifact dual-write which is SHADOW-active in the live b189d3cc0703 build -- RAW_DUALWRITE=true since T023, writing content-addressed raw bytes to a permanent R2 bucket within the free tier) and 3 HOLD (off and evidence/promotion-gated: the A1/A2 subnational sources in SHADOW, the S5 multi-board depth layer, and the S6 prediction models -- each proven in evidence but NOT deployed, so no unproven recurring spend). ## 2026-07-18 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.1 task ADP-S8-P01-T086 (production rollback & disaster-recovery drill; NOT_DEPLOYED)

- Eighty-sixth task (Stage S8, Release/Soak/Final Handoff) of the ADP V0.1 FINAL EXECUTION program. An ISOLATED production rollback & disaster-recovery drill across the six production components -- Worker, D1, R2, Source Registry, content bundle, prediction. For each, it identifies the recover-to KNOWN POINT and the recovery MECHANISM, PERFORMS the recovery in a throwaway sandbox (tmp dir / in-memory SQLite -- never issuing a live rollback or touching production D1/R2/network), measures RTO/RPO actuals + an evidence hash, and classifies any component that cannot be recovered to a consistent known state as a RELEASE BLOCKER. New tool arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/tools/disaster_recovery_drill.py reuses the committed pipeline tools (T029 restore_drill, T021 r2_artifact_key, T014 compile_registry, T018 render, T071 baselines) + the T085 committed anchors. Result: 6/6 components recover to a consistent known point with ZERO release blockers -- worker BUILD self-hash reproduces 452f7c5de919 (so any committed version is identifiable + integrity-verifiable and wrangler versions deploy can roll back to the live b189d3cc0703 == T040; actual live rollback NOT executed), D1 restores from the T027 open monthly snapshot into isolated in-memory SQLite (counts_consistent, 0 orphans, 329 versions across 3 months), R2 raw artifacts are content-addressed + immutable (identical bytes re-derive the identical key), the source registry recompiles to registry_hash d63cf6bd, the content bundle re-renders to a committed known-good hash, and prediction re-benchmarks to the committed report (forecast ledger append-only). RTO is the isolated-compute wall-time actual; RPO is 0 for every component (permanent/append-only or regenerable-from-permanent). release_mode NOT_DEPLOYED (no worker/schema/source_registry change; live still serves b189d3cc0703). Deliverables under evidence/ADP-S8-P01-T086/: dr_drill_report.json, rto_rpo_actuals.json, known_gaps.md (discloses the isolation boundary -- real canary rollback is T088, 14-day soak is T089 -- and that Cloudflare D1 Time Travel is not claimed), adversarial_review.md. Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S8-P01-T086/test-results/dr_drill_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0): the isolated drill completes and is consistent across all 6 components, 0 release blockers. Every component's recoverable compares the re-derivation to a COMMITTED known point (recovery_known_points.json for content_bundle/r2/d1, plus the committed registry_hash / worker build_id / baselines report) -- never a same-run self-comparison -- so a code/input drift flips it to a release blocker; a 4-lens adversarial review caught and fixed an initial content/r2 self-comparison vacuity. 3 load-bearing negative controls fire (flipping one source's enabled makes the registry recompile diverge from d63cf6bd; a content-bundle input drift makes the render hash diverge from b70fe73e; a different R2 content makes the key diverge from the committed key -- each flips recoverable False and is classified a release blocker; also the worker + registry source files are byte-immutable across the drill). Realtime not regressed (NOT deployed; live build b189d3cc0703). Cost (unknown != 0): production 0 (NOT_DEPLOYED, all local tmp/in-memory); 1 read-only GET. Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

A row-ledger records every count delta with a coded reason (items->docs -2 dedup; docs->versions +2 multi-item second versions; snapshot rows preserved). release_mode NOT_DEPLOYED (no worker/schema/source_registry change; live still serves b189d3cc0703 == T040). Deliverables under evidence/ADP-S8-P01-T085/: rehearsal_manifest.json, diff_report.json, data-samples/{items_500,fs_500}.json, known_gaps.md (discloses the scratchpad->committed fixture provenance, the prediction decoupling, and that production rollback/DR is T086 and 14-day soak is T089), adversarial_review.md. Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S8-P01-T085/test-results/rehearsal_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0): all 8 stages reproduce the committed anchors; no unexplained data loss; the 5 committed source-of-truth anchor files are byte-immutable across the replay; 3 load-bearing negative controls fire (dropping one input item breaks the canonical AND snapshot reproduction; a bogus live build flips production_untouched; a poisoned row-ledger is caught). Realtime not regressed (NOT deployed; live build b189d3cc0703). Cost (unknown != 0): production 0 (NOT_DEPLOYED, all in local tmp); 1 read-only GET. Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

## 2026-07-18 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.1 task ADP-S7-P04-T084 (evidence/inference + a11y + reduced-motion polish; NOT_DEPLOYED)

- Eighty-fourth task (the LAST S7 task) of the ADP V0.1 FINAL EXECUTION program. Polishes the professional information for clarity WITHOUT replacing the design. (1) Evidence vs inference: the item page rendered the 原文 (source/evidence) link and the generated 讲义 (lesson) sections with no marker, so a reader could mistake the auto-generated inference for the original; a const PROVENANCE_NOTE (a 讲义·推断 badge + a sentence saying the lesson is an auto-generated inference summary from the 原文, not the original) is now prepended in the CENTRAL lessonHTML(lesson) helper, so every lesson render (today/item/reveal/review) is labelled as inference, and the todayPage inline lesson render was refactored to call lessonHTML (DRY + the marker; output otherwise identical -- same section numbering + escaping). (2) Accessibility: the reveal button now carries aria-controls and, on click, moves focus INTO the revealed box (tabindex=-1) -- proper disclosure semantics; every interactive handler was already on a native focusable button/link with an accessible name, buttons are 44px (touch), and :focus-visible exists (T080). (3) Reduced-motion: verified the existing prefers-reduced-motion rule disables all animation/transition but RESTORES the animated content classes (.fr, .bw, both opacity:0 in HERO_CSS) to opacity:1, and the gauge/hero-video jump to their final state in JS -- so no content/function is lost (only the decorative .fx-cosmos meteor stays hidden). The polish lives entirely in page-body functions, so the six-theme visual/motion contract is BYTE-IDENTICAL; BUILD recomputed via its self-hash (d1dfcb3b7447 -> 452f7c5de919). release_mode NOT_DEPLOYED (live still serves b189d3cc0703). New tool arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/tools/a11y_content_audit.py. Deliverables under arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/evidence/ADP-S7-P04-T084/: browser_measurements.json (the 推断 marker renders, the reveal moves focus into the box, the grade buttons are keyboard-focusable, the reduced-motion CSSOM rule restores .fr/.bw), a11y_harness.html, pre_fix_worker.js, known_gaps.md (discloses the honest scoping -- the title's Diff view is the S5-T062 version-diff, not redone here -- and the reduced-motion/screen-reader test form) and adversarial_review.md. Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S7-P04-T084/test-results/a11y_content_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0): key tasks are keyboard/touch operable (native named buttons + focus moves into revealed content), evidence (原文 link) vs inference (讲义·推断 marker) is clearly distinguished (the pre-fix worker had no marker -- the check is discriminating), reduced-motion disables animation but restores the .fr/.bw content (removing the restore fails the check -- it is load-bearing), and the six-theme contract is byte-identical. ## 2026-07-18 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.1 task ADP-S7-P03-T083 (D1 query indexes + deterministic order; NOT_DEPLOYED)

- Eighty-third task of the ADP V0.1 FINAL EXECUTION program. Optimizes the hot D1 queries (today/radar/browse/history recency sort, lesson lookup, review due-queue, grade-history sparkline) by adding five indexes to deploy/cloudflare/schema_cloud.sql (all CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS, additive): idx_cn_items_recency ON cn_items(COALESCE(published_at,fetched_at) DESC, id DESC), idx_cn_items_board_recency ON cn_items(board_id, COALESCE(published_at,fetched_at) DESC, id DESC), idx_cn_lessons_item ON cn_lessons(item_id, created_at DESC), idx_cn_reviews_due ON cn_reviews(due_at) and idx_cn_events_kind_at ON cn_events(kind, at DESC). The busiest pages sort cn_items by COALESCE(published_at,fetched_at) DESC (the old fetched_at index could not serve it), so they were doing a full-table SCAN + a temporary B-tree sort of cn_items on every load; the expression index turns that into an index-ordered SEARCH that reads only the LIMIT rows (p95 down 3-200x in the local SQLite proof; recency scaling shows post-time flat while pre grows with N -> rows scanned O(N) -> O(LIMIT)). An independent adversarial review of the first (schema-only) cut found a real hole: without a total-order tie-breaker, on CROSS-FAMILY ties (a row whose recency comes from published_at ties on COALESCE with one whose recency comes from fetched_at), the board/browse LIMIT/OFFSET page membership and order changed pre-vs-post and OFFSET pagination could skip/repeat, and the verifier was blind to it (its synthetic published_at/fetched_at were in disjoint 2016/2026 namespaces so cross-family ties were impossible by construction). The fix adds a deterministic total-order tie-breaker `, id DESC` (`, i.id DESC` in the selection query) to all eight recency display ORDER BYs in worker_cloud.js -- matching the existing retention-prune query -- and puts the id tie-breaker in the two recency indexes so the total order is still fully index-served (no temp b-tree reintroduced); the verifier's synthetic data now contains real cross-family ties and asserts the tie-breaker query is deterministic (index result == forced full scan) with OFFSET pages disjoint. Because the queries changed, BUILD was recomputed via its self-hash (0cb3acee6bf3 -> d1dfcb3b7447); the query change lives in page-body functions, so the six-theme visual/motion contract is BYTE-IDENTICAL (no CLS -- the app is server-rendered), and this is NOT a content regression -- it makes a previously-undefined tie order deterministic. release_mode NOT_DEPLOYED (indexes apply at deploy; live still serves b189d3cc0703). CWV 达标 is NOT claimed (no field data; per the T081 rule). New tool arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/tools/db_query_plan.py. Deliverables under arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/evidence/ADP-S7-P03-T083/: query_plans.json (plans + p95 + scaling + cross-family-tie determinism), pre_fix_schema.sql, known_gaps.md (discloses the hole+fix, the index write-amplification cost and the honest scoping) and adversarial_review.md. Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S7-P03-T083/test-results/query_plan_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0): every hot query drops from SCAN + TEMP B-TREE to an index-ordered SEARCH with no temp b-tree, rows scanned O(N) -> O(LIMIT), the tie-breaker makes cross-family ties deterministic (index==forced-scan, OFFSET pages disjoint), all eight recency ORDER BYs carry the tie-breaker, and the six-theme contract is byte-identical. Realtime not regressed (NOT deployed; live build b189d3cc0703 == T040). Cost (unknown != 0): production 0 (NOT_DEPLOYED); on deploy the indexes add write-amplification on the daily-cron writes; 1 read-only GET. Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

## 2026-07-18 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.1 task ADP-S7-P03-T082 (ambient-motion performance without changing visual semantics; NOT_DEPLOYED)

- Eighty-second task of the ADP V0.1 FINAL EXECUTION program. Optimizes the six-theme ambient motion for FPS without changing its visual semantics. An audit of all ten @keyframes found nine already animate only compositor-safe properties (transform/opacity/filter); the single exception was the cosmos meteor keyframe, which animated left/top and thus forced layout+paint every frame. T082 converts it to transform:translate(112vw,56vh) rotate(18deg) -- SCREEN-PATH-EQUIVALENT because .fx is position:fixed;inset:0 (viewport-sized) and the .meteor base rule (left:-12%;top:8%;transform:rotate(18deg)) is unchanged, so left -12%->100% == translateX 0->112vw, top 8%->64% == translateY 0->56vh, with the rotate kept inner so the streak rotation and screen-space diagonal are preserved and the 0% keyframe equals the base transform (no jump). After the conversion EVERY ambient (infinite-loop) keyframe is compositor-safe -- the deterministic >=55 FPS guarantee (compositor animations do not drop main-thread frames). A router-injected FX_PERF_JS controller (in htmlResp, alongside RUM) pauses the ambient animation when the page is hidden (visibilitychange -> animationPlayState=paused on .fx children) and, on low-end devices (deviceMemory<=4 || hardwareConcurrency<=4 || saveData), sets data-fx-lite and degrades the heaviest layers (hides meteor/band, simplifies the nebula blur) while NEVER touching the foreground (component-state) selectors -- so the foreground feedback survives on low-end. The ONLY T077/T078 contract element that changed is `keyframes` (the meteor conversion); per_theme (all six themes incl. cosmos), base_css, theme_js, fx_css, reduced_motion and every hero element are byte-identical, and the change passes the T078 gate only as a documented approved change. release_mode NOT_DEPLOYED: BUILD recomputed via self-hash (8c19387c846b -> 0cb3acee6bf3) but NOT deployed -- live still serves b189d3cc0703. Deliverables under arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/evidence/ADP-S7-P03-T082/: before_after_trace.json (meteor layout True -> False + the equivalence derivation), browser_measurements.json (in-app browser: pause-when-hidden 7/7, and on low-end the meteor/band hide + nebula simplifies while the stars base ambience and the button:active foreground feedback survive), pre_fix_baseline.json, pre_fix_worker.js, known_gaps.md (discloses that a real median-FPS number needs a foregrounded browser -- the preview throttles rAF -- so the deterministic compositor-only guarantee is the load-bearing proof), and adversarial_review.md. Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S7-P03-T082/test-results/ambient_perf_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0): all seven ambient loops are compositor-safe (the pre-fix worker FAILS this -- meteor left/top -- so the audit discriminates), the low-end path degrades the heaviest layers while the foreground survives, pause-when-hidden works, and only `keyframes` changed on the contract (BLOCKs the gate without approval, PASS_APPROVED with one). Realtime not regressed (NOT deployed; live build b189d3cc0703 == T040). Cost (unknown != 0): production new_requests 0, D1 0, R2 0, model_calls 0, recurring cloud 0 (NOT_DEPLOYED); 1 read-only GET, 2 in-app-browser renders. Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

## 2026-07-18 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.1 task ADP-S7-P03-T081 (RUM / Core Web Vitals segmented by theme/route/device/network; NOT_DEPLOYED)

- Eighty-first task of the ADP V0.1 FINAL EXECUTION program. Instruments Real User Monitoring + Core Web Vitals (LCP/CLS/INP) segmented by theme/route/device/network. A RUM client (const RUM_JS) uses PerformanceObserver for LCP (largest-contentful-paint), CLS (layout-shift excluding hadRecentInput) and INP (approximated as the max interaction event duration -- disclosed as an approximation, not spec INP), tags each metric with the theme (documentElement data-theme), route (pathname normalized), device (viewport-width bucket) and network (navigator.connection.effectiveType), and sends them via navigator.sendBeacon('/api/rum') on visibilitychange->hidden / pagehide. The client is injected at the ROUTER level (inside htmlResp, behind RUM_ENABLED), so it touches NO T077/T078 visual/motion contract hash -- the entire asset_hashes dict (all 6 per-theme + all 11 motion elements + page_shell + master_visual) is BYTE-IDENTICAL. A pure rumIngest(payload, roll) validator (metric allowlist, per-metric value range, sampling, theme/device allowlist, route/network sanitization) gates the new POST /api/rum endpoint, which CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS cn_rum + a bind()-parameterized INSERT (a NEW table, never existing production data). The offline query tool arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/tools/rum_cwv.py computes p75 and rates LCP/INP/CLS against Google thresholds, segmentable by theme/route/device/network (query / query_multi / overall_baseline), with EVERY assessment gated on a minimum sample count -- below the gate it returns insufficient_data with no rating, so an empty or thin dataset claims NO compliance (the '无数据不声称达标' rule). release_mode NOT_DEPLOYED: BUILD recomputed via self-hash (40a46aa2baee -> 8c19387c846b) but NOT deployed -- live still serves b189d3cc0703; there is NO real RUM baseline yet and none is claimed. Deliverables under arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/evidence/ADP-S7-P03-T081/: browser_measurements.json (in-app browser: the real client captured a live LCP=2128ms + CLS + INP tagged by all four dimensions and beaconed to /api/rum), test-results/rum_ingest_test.js (Node test on the REAL extracted rumIngest -- bad metric/value/payload/oversized/sampled-out all rejected before any D1 write), pre_fix_baseline.json, pre_fix_worker.js, known_gaps.md (discloses the INP approximation + the per-page-view D1 write cost + the sampling lever), and adversarial_review.md. The two grade() client flows are rewritten as an optimistic UNDO window: a click shows the picked grade + an 撤销 button + a 4s cancelable countdown and fires NO write; the /api/grade POST fires only in a deferred gradeCommit() after the window, and gradeUndo() cancels the timer and writes nothing (so an undo touches no production data, honouring the rollback rule); grade commit and run() also gain try/catch -> [data-state=err] error states (previously a failed fetch hung the UI). Theme switch preserves state because applyTheme() only setAttribute('data-theme') + syncs hero/gauge -- no reload/navigate/innerHTML rebuild. ## 2026-07-17 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.1 task ADP-S6-P03-T075 (Shadow topic-acceleration & central->local diffusion prediction; SHADOW)

- Seventy-fifth task of the ADP V0.1 FINAL EXECUTION program. Two PREDEFINED pilot targets over the 2016+ event chain, each with a DISTINCT fixture (not clones): ACCEL-PILOT (will a research topic accelerate within 90 days?, base rate ~0.5) and DIFFUSION-A0-A1 (will a central A0 policy diffuse to a province A1 within 180 days?, base rate ~0.6). Each prediction conditions on a leading net support signal (support - counter, e.g. how many A1 provinces already echo the A0 policy minus superseding central events); the conditional model beats an unconditional base-rate baseline over three time-safe rolling windows whose validation is deliberately NOISY (carries impurities, so the model is imperfect and wins on aggregate not by construction), and every surfaced statement is a hedged probability -- no deterministic tone. release_mode SHADOW; predictions are computed in the dev/shadow environment only, the production worker/cron/data untouched, 0 cloud cost, DIR-007 unaffected, and the realtime build is unchanged. Deliverables under arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/evidence/ADP-S6-P03-T075/: diffusion_predictor_report.json, known_gaps.md, and adversarial_review.md (review CONFIRMED_SOUND after a HOLE_FOUND on a vacuous control was fixed). Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S6-P03-T075/test-results/diffusion_predictor_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0), the verifier re-deriving each window's Brier with its own formula: three windows beat the baseline for both pilots (ACCEL 0.163/0.179/0.161 vs 0.250/0.258/0.250; DIFFUSION 0.169/0.146/0.137 vs 0.278/0.262/0.257 -- distinct profiles), with a REAL feature-ablation control (signal-blinded cases collapse the model exactly onto the baseline, ties, does not beat) and a corrupted-signal probe (inverting the validation signal degrades the model to 0.46-0.56, far worse than baseline) proving the win comes from the support/counter signal not the harness; the targets and horizon are predefined (a post-hoc target is refused by both is_predefined and rolling_backtest); and no deterministic tone (all surfaced probabilities strictly inside (0,1), and the gate rejects certainty phrasing and 0/1 probabilities). Realtime not regressed (no production deploy, live build b189d3cc0703 == T040). Cost (unknown != 0): production new_requests 0, D1 0, R2 0, model_calls 0, recurring cloud 0 (SHADOW dev env). Predicts whether an official source's current quiet is abnormal (it should have published by now) or normal (within its cadence), and distinguishes abnormal source silence from a collection failure (our fetcher broke). release_mode SHADOW; predictions are computed in the dev/shadow environment only, the production worker/cron/data untouched, 0 cloud cost, DIR-007 unaffected, and the realtime build is unchanged. Deliverables under arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/evidence/ADP-S6-P03-T074/: silence_predictor_report.json, known_gaps.md, and adversarial_review.md (review CONFIRMED_SOUND). ## 2026-07-17 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.1 task ADP-S6-P01-T070 (Dataset Snapshot + observed_at leakage guard; NOT_DEPLOYED)

Ensures 2026-backfilled old files cannot pretend to have been known at a historical point in time: a dataset snapshot is keyed on observed_at (when ADP actually fetched a document), never on doc_date (when the policy issued), so a 2016 policy observed only in 2026 is not in a 2018 snapshot. release_mode NOT_DEPLOYED; a read-only library, the production worker/cron/data untouched. Reuses T056 coverage_asof._parse_date. Deliverables under arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/evidence/ADP-S6-P01-T070/: dataset_snapshot_report.json, known_gaps.md, and adversarial_review.md (review CONFIRMED_SOUND). Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S6-P01-T070/test-results/dataset_snapshot_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0): a clean as-of snapshot passes the leakage guard, while EXTERNALLY injecting a future-observed doc, a 2026-backfilled doc, or a doc with no observed_at each RAISES (so injecting a future document makes the test fail); the snapshot is observed_at-keyed, not doc_date-keyed (a backfilled doc whose doc_date 2016-05-01 is before the 2018 as_of but whose observed_at is 2026-07-01 is excluded, so the 2018 snapshot is exactly [a, b]); and any prediction can rebuild its dataset (rebuild_for_prediction reproduces the snapshot_id, is order-independent and reproducible, and a later as_of expands the dataset). - Sixty-second task of the ADP V0.1 FINAL EXECUTION program (S5-P02). Adds the user-facing read layer over the document version chain: a version timeline, a locatable old-vs-new diff, an as-of history query, and old-version replay -- so a user can SEE the real change, the historical state, and the source location. release_mode NOT_DEPLOYED; a read-only API library, the production worker/cron/data untouched. New tool arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/tools/version_asof_api.py: version_timeline (folds renders into SUBSTANTIVE versions -- a noise-only re-render never becomes a version -- each carrying its noise-stripped body snapshot), diff_payload (a line-level LOCATABLE diff classifying every change add/delete/modify with its line number and exact text, computed over the noise-stripped body so TEMPLATE NOISE IS NEVER SHOWN), as_of (the version in force as of a date, by parsed date, NEVER a future version -- reuses T056), and replay_version / replay_is_idempotent (deterministic reconstruction of an OLD version, idempotent across replays). Reuses T026 version_engine (noise rules + version decision) and T056 coverage_asof (as-of resolver) rather than re-implementing them. Deliverables under arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/evidence/ADP-S5-P02-T062/: version_asof_report.json, known_gaps.md, and adversarial_review.md (review CONFIRMED_SOUND). Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S5-P02-T062/test-results/version_asof_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0): a substantive v2-vs-v1 diff is exactly {add:1, delete:1, modify:1} each located to its line with the correct old/new text; a noise-only re-render yields an EMPTY diff and adds no version, while a raw un-stripped diff of the SAME pair surfaces 6 noise lines (proving the stripping is load-bearing); real article text is never stripped; an old version replays byte-for-byte and is idempotent over 3 runs; and as_of never returns a future version -- 0 future-leakage and 0 oracle-disagreements over a 288-sample battery, while a deliberately-future resolver is caught on 70 samples. Realtime not regressed (no deploy, live build b189d3cc0703 == T040). Cost (unknown != 0): production new_requests 0, D1 0, R2 0, model_calls 0. ## 2026-07-17 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.1 task ADP-S2-P03-T030 (orchestration cost decision + idempotency; closes S2; NOT_DEPLOYED)

- Thirtieth task of the ADP V0.1 FINAL EXECUTION program and the LAST of S2 (Durable Evidence & Versioning). Goal: compare Cron+Queue with Workflows and decide whether to introduce added complexity. NOT_DEPLOYED, 0 recurring cloud cost; a decision plus a reliability/cost experiment, no production orchestration change. Deliverables under arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/: tools/idempotency_harness.py (a deterministic at-least-once channel + idempotent processor + dead-letter queue that proves exactly-once effect, plus an operation-cost benchmark across the three candidate paths) and ORCHESTRATION_ADR.md. Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S2-P03-T030/test-results/orchestration_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0): the at-least-once envelope and DLQ are exercised (40 logical tasks, 55 deliveries with real duplicates, 36 effects each applied exactly once, 4 poison messages all routed to the DLQ, no effect applied twice); the cost benchmark distinguishes the free path from the paid paths and encodes DIR-007 (Path A, Cron + in-worker idempotent + a D1 retry/DLQ ledger, is free and DIR-007-ok with zero queue operations and zero workflow steps; Path B with Cloudflare Queues and Path C with Cloudflare Workflows both require the Workers Paid plan and add roughly 1170 queue operations or 480 workflow steps per month, so both are DIR-007-blocked); and the decision keeps the simple path. DECISION: keep the free Cron + idempotent + D1 retry/DLQ path and do NOT adopt Queues or Workflows -- both require leaving the Free tier (forbidden by DIR-007 without explicit Owner authorization) and add per-operation and per-step cost and maintenance with no reliability gain at one cron per day, since the free path already yields exactly-once effect; revisit only on a real reliability gap AND explicit Owner paid authorization. This closes Stage S2 (raw evidence, canonical documents, version chains, open snapshots, recovery, and orchestration cost). Cost (unknown != 0): new_requests 0, D1 0, R2 0, model_calls 0. Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

Goal: export the canonical documents and their append-only version chains as a monthly-partitioned open columnar snapshot (real Apache Parquet) plus a hashed manifest, for large-scale historical analysis, recovery, and backtestable prediction. NOT_DEPLOYED, 0 recurring cloud cost; the snapshot is generated offline from a D1 sample and touches no production D1, R2, or worker. Deliverables under arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/: tools/snapshot_writer.py (derives two typed logical tables -- cn_documents and cn_document_versions -- from a D1 sample via the T024 canonicalizer and the T026 version engine, partitions each by month, writes real Parquet via pyarrow with a deterministic NDJSON fallback, carries a versioned SCHEMA_REGISTRY with a backward-compatible evolve_schema, and emits a snapshot_manifest), SNAPSHOT_SPEC.md, and schemas/snapshot_manifest.schema.json. Reproducibility is anchored on a format- and engine-independent logical_hash (a Parquet stream embeds the writer version, so physical bytes only match within one engine version); the manifest records both the logical_hash and the physical_sha256. Acceptance verified over the real 500-item D1 sample (evidence/ADP-S2-P03-T027/test-results/snapshot_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0): the snapshot is 498 canonical documents / 500 versions / 46 months (2016-01..2026-07) / 92 partitions; the same logical snapshot regenerates identically (equal snapshot_id, equal per-partition logical_hash, and equal physical Parquet bytes in-environment); the D1 sample and the Parquet are row- and relationship-consistent (498 document rows and 500 version rows read back from Parquet match the sample-derived tables, every version's canonical_id resolves to a document with zero orphans, and every row lands in the correct month partition); and schema evolution is backward compatible (adding a nullable column lets an old v1 partition still read with the new column null-filled while the v1 logical_hash stays stable). The committed logical_snapshot/*.jsonl recomputes all 92 manifest logical_hashes offline without pyarrow, and the manifest validates against its draft-07 schema. A dev dependency pyarrow==17.0.0 was installed into the user's Python 3.9 user-site to emit real Parquet; it is an offline evidence dependency the runtime/worker do not use, and the writer falls back to deterministic NDJSON with the identical logical_hash when it is absent. Cost (unknown != 0): new_requests 0, D1 0, R2 0, model_calls 0. Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

## 2026-07-16 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.1 task ADP-S2-P02-T026 (version diff + template-noise filter + replay idempotency; NOT_DEPLOYED)

- Twenty-sixth task of the ADP V0.1 FINAL EXECUTION program and the last of S2-P02 (Canonical Document and version chain), one task per run. Goal: append a DocumentVersion only for a substantive change; never inflate the version chain for template noise; and make ingestion idempotent so any task can be safely replayed. NOT_DEPLOYED, 0 recurring cloud cost; rules-only, no worker, D1, or R2 change (the engine is not yet wired into the write path). Deliverables under arxiv-daily-push/docs/pursuing_goal/v0_1/: tools/version_engine.py (strip_noise for template chrome; a substantive signature = the noise-stripped body hash + the sorted attachment content-hash set + the status; content_hash over that signature; a diff that explains whether the body, attachments, or status changed or the change was noise-only; an append-only ingest that adds a version only when the content_hash differs from the tip and is idempotent on replay; and a replay check that runs a sequence N times and requires identical chains), VERSION_ENGINE_SPEC.md, and NOISE_RULES.md (a conservative Chinese-site boilerplate ruleset). Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S2-P02-T026/test-results/version_tests.txt, ACCEPTANCE = PASS, exit 0): a footer/nav/share/engagement-count/relative-timestamp/copyright/ICP change is noise-only and adds no version; a body correction, an added attachment (body unchanged), and a status change (body and attachments unchanged) each add exactly one version, giving a clean append-only v1..v4 with four distinct content hashes; three replays of the sequence are byte-identical and re-ingesting the current tip does not grow the chain; and the CLI is deterministic across runs. Two real defects were found and fixed while implementing: a \b word boundary after a CJK alternative never fires between two CJK characters (so a share-widget line survived), and a greedy timestamp rule would have silently deleted a real sentence that merely begins with a publish verb and a colon -- both are documented in NOISE_RULES.md with guard tests. Cost (unknown != 0): new_requests 0, D1 0, R2 0, model_calls 0. Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

## 2026-07-16 Australia/Sydney - ADP V0.1 task ADP-S2-P01-T023 (capped R2 shadow + cost/performance report; SHADOW)

- Twenty-third task of the ADP V0.1 FINAL EXECUTION program (S2-P01), one task per run. Goal: before extending history, measure the save completeness, latency, and real extrapolated cost. release_mode SHADOW. The shadow surfaced a DIR-007 free-tier constraint: the naive per-feed dual-write (a D1 read + R2 head + R2 put + D1 write per feed, over ~13 concurrent feeds) exceeded the Cloudflare free-tier Worker subrequest limit (~50/request), so those writes were silently dropped (no budget harm; feeds still parsed and published). Fixed with a per-run write cap (RAW_MAX_PER_RUN=3), reading the budget snapshot once per run instead of per write, and resetting the counter at runDaily start and each selftest, keeping the extra subrequests within the free tier. Change to deploy/cloudflare/worker_cloud.js; deployed the capped shadow adp-cloud version 64c8b842 (build 9cd3d8a2fe68, RAW_DUALWRITE=true), six themes 6/6 intact on both domains. Acceptance verified (evidence/ADP-S2-P01-T023/test-results/shadow_verify.txt): the writer's save/hash/readback are 100% -- the R2 object is content-addressed (the key sha256 equals the content sha256), a readback via wrangler r2 object get --remote returns the exact 76 bytes whose sha256 equals the key (integrity 100%), and a repeated write dedups to a single object and a single D1 row (idempotent); the dual-write is capped and subrequest-safe and never blocks parse or publish (a p95 delta over real feed batches accrues via the daily cron, since a fresh manual run is blocked today by the once-per-day guard); and the cost extrapolation is within the free-tier budget -- <=3 Class A writes / <=3 Class B heads / <=150KB per run, i.e. <=90 Class A / <=90 Class B / <=4.5 MB per month, about 0.009% / 0.045% of the free tier with a recurring delta of ~$0. The gate criteria (save/hash/readback 100%, cost within budget, subrequest constraint fixed) are met, so entering the version migration (S2-P02) is safe; the literal 7-day / 1000-artifact accumulation runs via cron over real time. PARAM-ADP-1124 re-attested unchanged as adp-v03-j5-cloud-v13; TRACEABILITY_MATRIX / VERSION_MATRIX / delivery_tasks updated. Rollback: wrangler versions deploy 657fe32a (T022, flag off = no dual-write). Ends IMPLEMENTATION_READY_FOR_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION.

## 2026-07-15 Australia/Sydney - Self-hosted the hero videos (removed the external CloudFront dependency)

- The hero videos were still loading from an external CloudFront that is decaying (one clip already dead). The Owner authorized fixing this but does not want to touch the dashboard, and Cloudflare R2 (the v1.1 recommendation) needs a one-time dashboard enable that is a billing/terms action, so it was not taken on the Owner's behalf. Instead the three still-live clips were self-hosted on the Worker via Cloudflare static assets: downloaded and compressed with ffmpeg (obtained through the pip package imageio-ffmpeg, no system install) to 1280x720 H.264 no-audio loops (62MB down to 7MB total, also far lighter on mobile), stored under deploy/cloudflare/assets/media, served same-origin at /media/*.mp4 via a wrangler assets binding. HERO_VIDEO now points at /media/*.mp4 and the CSP media-src is back to 'self' with CloudFront removed entirely, so the site has zero external media dependency and the videos are durable with the deployment. The mp4 files were force-added past the repo's media/ gitignore because durability requires them versioned. Live-verified: all three /media clips serve 200 video/mp4 same-origin and the hero video plays. cosmos keeps its dashboard (its own source clip was already dead).

Live-verified per theme in a fresh no-cache tab: the minimal, techno and forest videos actually play, and the cosmos gauge animated to 094. Note: the reference videos are external and one is already dead, so they should be moved to owner storage (R2) for durability.

## 2026-07-15 Australia/Sydney - Made theme motion boldly visible + fixed the cache hiding every deploy

- After the previous change the Owner still saw no motion on both computer and phone, even on a fresh URL. Two root causes, both fixed in deploy/cloudflare/worker_cloud.js. (1) Cache: DOM inspection proved the browser was serving a fully cached page (computed card background still 0.58 and band animation 90s -- the OLD css) despite cache-control: no-cache; these browsers store no-cache responses and skip revalidation, so the Owner had not actually received any recent deploy. Changed the HTML cache-control from no-cache to no-store, must-revalidate so browsers always refetch (confirmed live). This is the main reason updates were invisible. (2) Visibility: the ambient effects were technically rendering but far too faint (1px stars, off-screen nebulae) because the original design leaned on full-screen hero videos that were not ported. Amplified the self-contained CSS: cosmos now has on-screen nebula-glow backgrounds, a conic aurora sweep, brighter and denser twinkling stars, and a 6-second glowing meteor, with cosmos cards made translucent (0.40) so the galaxy shows through; techno clouds are larger and brighter; minimal gains a moving light shaft; forest slopes are taller with a slow sway. Verified in a fresh no-cache browser tab: the cosmos galaxy and techno clouds are now clearly visible.

## 2026-07-15 Australia/Sydney - Restored the six-theme ambient motion layers

- Owner: "the 6 themes just change one color now, the original motion/animation design is all gone -- don't fix A and lose B." Correct: the Stage 2 six-theme port into deploy/cloudflare/worker_cloud.js had copied only the colour tokens and layout and dropped every per-theme animated layer that the local design source src/adp/templates/base.html defines. Restored them faithfully as pure CSS/SVG (no external dependency, CSP-safe), driven by a THEME_FX map and a data-fx attribute (set in the no-flash head-init and applyTheme, validated and self-healing like the theme guard): cosmos regains the galaxy layer (a slowly drifting light band, three nebula glows, two twinkling star fields, and an 11-second shooting meteor); techno regains three drifting white fluid clouds; minimal regains the ocean top-light and deep radial vignette; forest regains the layered hill-slope SVG and the water band; plus a gentle card fade-in entrance and a prefers-reduced-motion guard that disables the motion. warm and fresh stay clean (no fx) exactly as the original design intends. The external CloudFront hero videos from base.html were intentionally not ported (CSP and dependency fragility; the CSS ambient layers carry the motion). Content stays above the layers via z-index (fx at z-index 0, pointer-events none). Live-verified per theme on adp.linzezhang.com at both desktop and phone width, with the ChatGPT deep-dive button and the theme self-heal intact.

## 2026-07-15 Australia/Sydney - Theme-selector self-heal hotfix

- Owner reported the webpage's 6 themes were gone and would not come back. Reproduced in-browser: the six-theme picker read the stored theme from localStorage and applied it without validating, so a stale/invalid stored value (from an earlier build) or an Object.prototype key such as 'constructor'/'__proto__'/'toString' set an invalid data-theme (no matching CSS -> page fell back to the default warm palette) and left the native <select> at selectedIndex -1 (blank switcher). To the Owner this looked exactly like all 6 themes had vanished and their chosen theme was not restored. Fix (deploy/cloudflare/worker_cloud.js): the no-flash head-init and the theme script now validate the stored value with Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(THEMES, s) (an isTheme() helper) and fall back to 'warm' unless it is one of the six, and applyTheme rewrites the corrected value so a bad entry self-heals on first load. Live-verified on adp.linzezhang.com: stored 'aurora' and 'constructor' both self-heal to warm (switcher shows 暖纸学习), and picking 森林河流 persists across page navigation.

## 2026-07-15 Australia/Sydney - ChatGPT deep-dive button + local cleanup

- Owner: "delete useless local info; add a jump to ChatGPT so it can traverse the whole web, think and search deeply, give me some surprises, and explain the corresponding content in a detailed, professional, comprehensive, deep way." Feature (deploy/cloudflare/worker_cloud.js): every daily pick, item-detail page, and review card now shows a "让 ChatGPT 全网深度追问" button that opens ChatGPT (chatgpt.com/?hints=search&q=) with a prompt pre-filled from that item's title, authors, categories, original link, and abstract, instructing ChatGPT to do a live deep web search (cross-checked with citable sources), reason deeply about the problem/method/assumptions/innovation/limits, give a detailed and professional and comprehensive and deep explanation for someone who wants to truly learn it, surface some surprises (unexpected links, counter-intuitive conclusions, overlooked angles), and end with a "what to read/do next" list; the search page also gets a topic deep-dive button. The rendered href is escaped (encodeURIComponent leaves only the literal & to become &amp;), so there is no injection surface. Live-verified on adp.linzezhang.com across today/item/review/search with the decoded prompt correct. Local cleanup (no tracked-file change): the retired mirror/tunnel architecture no longer backs adp.linzezhang.com, so the dormant com.linze.adp.web (uvicorn 8787) and com.linze.adp.tunnel (cloudflared) LaunchAgents were unloaded and their installed plists, the cloudflared connector token, the 38MB local cloudflared binary, and dead logs removed; the reinstall templates stay under deploy/cloudflare/launchd/, and the site still serves 200 on every route afterward, confirming the local residue was unused.
